Furthermore, a major war could also lead to a global pandemic, as Bill Gates, billionaire philanthropist and entrepreneur, has warned [3]. The world would be plunged into chaos, with nations struggling to cope with the devastating effects of war and disease.

The impact on the global economy would be immense, with a potential global war leading to a full-scale war in the Gulf, further inflaming radical Islam and seeking to inflict further damage on the U.S. and Israel, or the Gulf monarchies they view as Washington toadies [1]. The economic consequences of this scenario are awful, with oil prices spiking higher and the dollar continuing to weaken [1]. The economic consequences of this scenario are awful, with oil prices spiking higher and the dollar continuing to weaken [1]. In this scenario, the Fed would be in a bind, having to keep rates higher than it otherwise would like to offset possible inflationary pressures from a weaker dollar [1].
